commit 3a0e1eb08b381b9a3041d55dde7c60b5fa0485d9
Author: Adam Preble <adam.preble@gmail.com>
Date:   2018-05-15 16:32:42 -0400

    The testing Python log cleanser now skips Pycharm debugger messages.
    
    When debugging unit tests in PyCharm, the stdout starts with a preamble:
    pydev debugger: process [PID] is connecting
    
    Where [PID] is the numeric ID. This will fail the diff against the Java
    reference models. This adds an additional filter to existing filter logic to
    strip that message.

commit f77349274a021fc069687a2af95a58d2d96adad9
Author: Adam Preble <adam.preble@gmail.com>
Date:   2018-05-15 16:32:42 -0400

    The testing Python log cleanser now skips Pycharm debugger messages.
    
    When debugging unit tests in PyCharm, the stdout starts with a preamble:
    pydev debugger: process [PID] is connecting
    
    Where [PID] is the numeric ID. This will fail the diff against the Java
    reference models. This adds an additional filter to existing filter logic to
    strip that message.

Author: Tzu-ping Chung <uranusjr@gmail.com>
Date:   2017-06-23 10:05:12 +0800

    Refactor Slice to delay type checking
    
    slice() literally accepts *anything* as its arguments, and does not
    check for types until it's applied to a sequence. This refactors the
    constructor and attributes to match this fact, and provide an extra
    method (and inner class) for its callee to perform type checking.

commit 887ce779563bec9b40733fe5e2fa5ffea53e4d52
Author: Tzu-ping Chung <uranusjr@gmail.com>
Date:   2017-06-12 12:30:32 +0800

    Handle return statements inside non-if structures
    
    An implicit reutrn is required in a Python function even when there is
    an explicit return, if the statement is inside a nested structure
    (loop, condition, or try-catch block).
    
    This commit adds a property that calculates whether there is a nested
    structure inside a block, and use it to determine whether the block
    needs an extra implicit return statement when visiting the explicit one.
    
    The same logic is added to the visit_Lambda as well.
    
    Fixes #533.

6	0	voc/python/blocks.py
1	1	voc/python/methods.py

commit 578491879beafb8d62daad6c64ebb971177a98fd
Author: Chiang Fong Lee <myself@cflee.net>
Date:   2017-05-23 22:42:38 +0800

    Patch rich comparisons to handle Types
    
    - The implementation I did in #122 assumes that when calling
    __getattribute_null() on an operand to dynamically obtain the method, it
    always returns a Method, which can be duly invoked for a result.
    - However, this assumption is faulty for org.python.types.Type operands
    (`type(1)`), as its __getattribute_null() returns a Function which isnt
    already bound to an object instance.
    - In any case it only makes sense to invoke the comparison method on an
    object, not on a class/type, so just avoid this entirely by testing if
    its a Method thats already bound to an object instance.

1	1	python/common/org/python/types/Object.java

commit 49c58b657f8953b1b6fe233309f4720fc3df30d6
Author: Elias Dorneles <eliasdorneles@gmail.com>
Date:   2017-02-06 23:04:01 -0200

    fix maximum stack size for an edge case
    The bytecode generated for the test case added in this commit
    reaches the limit of the stack size, see the ASM analysis here:
    
    https://gist.github.com/eliasdorneles/742ccff84a0474e6904a369293ab1dd9
    
    In the max_stack value calculation, len(self.parameters) was 0,
    so that max_stack ends up with value 8.
    
    Looking at the ASM analysis linked above, one can see that it
    reaches the limit, and even though the INVOKESTATIC function
    would consume 1 element from the stack (the argument) before
    adding its result to the stack, this seems to not be enough.

commit 45703f0acf774b5e656516d56d015ee2b632a3da
Author: Chiang Fong Lee <myself@cflee.net>
Date:   2017-01-15 21:02:39 +0800

    Add end of code canary print to detect early termination
    
    - Used to detect unexpected early termination, especially due to
    exceptions.
    - Tests should handle exceptions where possible, printing out the
    accompanying error message.
    - Otherwise, the exits_early flag can be set on assertCodeExecution() to
    disable the canary check, preferably with a `print(Done.)` statement
    at the end of the code block to detect any difference in handling
    between Python and Java implementations.
    - Enabling exits_early flag but still having the output end with the
    canary should fail as well.

commit 48ae03bf125e35f29e662b5d461d4cd76aadb9b8
Author: Sjoerd Job Postmus <sjoerdjob@sjec.nl>
Date:   2016-06-17 01:25:51 +0200

    Register tempdir cleanup procedure before creating temp dir.
    
    Between creating the temporary directory and finally registering the
    cleanup procedure was a significant amount of code. Any exception (or
    just me pressing CTRL-C out of boredom) would leave behind another stale
    tmpdir.
    
    By reordering the logic, the cleanup of the test directory is a bit more
    robust.

commit 5855a594dac16e9106f1266ad9cb8f79ec481876
Author: Sjoerd Job Postmus <sj.postmus@developers.nl>
Date:   2016-06-15 16:28:10 +0200

4	1	tests/utils.py

commit deecfa95b97dc5f2c512935a5c8698b1b686b4af
Author: Sjoerd Job Postmus <sj.postmus@developers.nl>
Date:   2016-06-15 07:50:33 +0200

    Respect @expectedFailure when processing `not_implemented`.
    
    During the processing of `not_implemented`, the value of
    `__unittest_expecting_failure__` was enforced, instead of marking it
    when not already set.
    
    Also, it turns out that the marker was set on the method, which was
    shared among different testcases. The marker should instead be set on
    the instance of the `TestCase`, which makes sure it is only remembered
    for that specific run.

16	46	tests/utils.py

commit 1bc3d2637ecde94f2c680f4ba8295015da945bec
Author: Petr Viktorin <encukou@gmail.com>
Date:   2016-06-05 15:49:12 -0700

    Implement float.__repr__
    
    This is a *very* simplified version of what CPython does in
    PyOS_double_to_string: use native string formatting and then fix it
    up.
    There are edge cases where this does not give the same result
    as CPython's float.__repr__, but it should never be *wrong*.
    
    This removes the need to normalize floats in the test output,
    and it fixes the float modulo tests.

    Implement reflected operations

    and stub out on BaseException and Super.
    - Implement `comparison(other, operator)` on org.python.types.Object,
    instead of directly in bytecode, as it's a little complex and it's
    difficult to do this without storing local variables in the JVM.
    - Change COMPARE_OP opcode to invoke the new helper method.
    - This fixes most of the tests that the direct-call datatype comparison
    method changes broke.

commit cad53da15e1d629027dd14fbb688af4246da6e66
Author: Chiang Fong Lee <myself@cflee.net>
Date:   2016-03-30 13:47:14 +0800

    Fix JAVA_STACK regex consuming trailing spaces
    
    - This was breaking tests for exception messages that end with one or
    more trailing spaces, as they accidentally get 'stripped' off as part of
    the \s special sequence which includes newlines and spaces.
    - Instead, use the MULTILINE mode, start the regex with ^ to match each
    newline, and then include the EOL at the back with `\r?\n` to ensure
    that it is not left behind in the exception string after replacing.

1	1	tests/utils.py

commit 87005e0b51a5bbd17c42e09817acb2179132c705
Author: Chiang Fong Lee <myself@cflee.net>
Date:   2016-03-21 22:59:55 +0800

    Fix race condition between compile and testdaemon startup
    
    - As `setUpClass()` is runs before `setUp()`, ensure that the defined
    `setUpSuite()` which runs `ant java` to build the jars is run before
    testdaemon is started up.
    - This was not an issue before the introduction of testdaemon because
    only `setUp()` was defined.
    - This should fix some spurious build pass/fail results due to the old
    python-java.jar being used on testdaemon startup, before ant completes
    the build.

commit fc9a76ea8f07c9213da43485f4c690f997410c71
Author: Chiang Fong Lee <myself@cflee.net>
Date:   2016-03-18 15:50:49 +0800

    Switch to using Thread's ContextClassLoader
    
    - This is primarily to allow org.python.ImportLib to use the newl
    JoinClassLoader in TestDaemon to load the new tests/temp/ classes.
    Otherwise, it uses the ImportLib class' classloader, which is the
    previous test case's classloader, which has the wrong set of classes for
    tests/temp/.
    - There should be no impact under non-testing circumstances as nobody
    should be messing with the running Thread's ContextClassLoader.
    - Fixes test cases which only work correctly on the first run, and which
    may not work correctly for subsequent runs if the underlying classes are
    replaced.

commit 58466e972187aefa85b3a4b1386bea863e79fb1c
Author: Chiang Fong Lee <myself@cflee.net>
Date:   2016-03-17 14:29:33 +0800

    Fix testdaemon issues when additional classes are defined
    
    - Previously, classes in python-java.jar (in particular
    org.python.types.Type) were having issues loading the transpiled classes
    . This is due to the python-java.jar classes being loaded by the default
    AppClassLoader, which can't see the transpiled classes, as that
    classloader is the "parent" of our URLClassLoader.
    - Fix this by loading that jar in our URLClassLoader instead of the
    `java -classpath` command.

commit 37dd47e6a087929936b26aa1ce7666466247a5d4
Author: Chiang Fong Lee <myself@cflee.net>
Date:   2016-03-16 16:03:10 +0800

    Switch to using testdaemon for runAsJava()
    
    - Use subprocess.stdin and .stdout instead of .communicate, because the
    latter waits for the process to reply and exit.
    - Since we can't receive an EOF from testdaemon (that would require
    closing System.out, which can't be opened), and it's difficult to
    determine if the output is done, we sense for a ".\n" line that
    testdaemon specially sends to signal this.
    - Need to flush subprocess.stdin, otherwise things just hang there.

Author: Chiang Fong Lee <myself@cflee.net>
Date:   2016-03-11 10:36:04 +0800

    Switch int binary eq/ne default to false
    
    - This fixes tuple, list (and range if it was implemented) because they
    can only be compared for equality within their types.
    - Dicts require equal (key, value) pairs to be equal, which doesn't
    exist in int. Putting the int into the keys or values of a dict doesn't
    seem to make it equal either.
    - Strings seem to be not equal with int.
    - Sets seem to be not equal with int.

    Modified handling of modules to prevent namespace collisions.
    
    The JVM allows for foo.class and foo/bar.class (i.e., a class with the same name as a package)
    but the Java compiler doesn't. Since Android needs to compile some sources, even if it's
    pure VOC, the old scheme posed a problem.
